The flow works as follows:\\n\\n**1. Configuration Definition (prometheus/prometheus/config/config.go)**\\nPrometheus defines TLS configuration in multiple config structures:\\n- ScrapeConfig (line 747): HTTPClientConfig inline field for scrape targets\\n- RemoteWriteConfig (line 1419): HTTPClientConfig inline field (line 1434) for remote write endpoints\\n- RemoteReadConfig (line 1587): HTTPClientConfig inline field (line 1597) for remote read endpoints\\n- AlertmanagerConfig (line 1300): HTTPClientConfig inline field (line 1305) for alertmanager communication\\n- TracingConfig (line 1160): Direct TLSConfig field (line 1165) for tracing endpoints\\n\\nAll HTTPClientConfig structs (from prometheus-common) contain an embedded TLSConfig field that defines certificates, CA files, server names, and other TLS settings.\\n\\n**2. Scrape Targets (prometheus/prometheus/scrape/scrape.go)**\\nAt line 155 in newScrapeLoop, the scrape client is created from ScrapeConfig.HTTPClientConfig:\\n  client, err := newScrapeClient(cfg.HTTPClientConfig, cfg.JobName, options.HTTPClientOptions...)\\n\\nAt line 2260-2261, newScrapeClient delegates to prometheus-common:\\n  func newScrapeClient(cfg config_util.HTTPClientConfig, name string, ...) Discovery Service Clients (prometheus/prometheus/discovery/)**\\nMany discovery modules use HTTPClientConfig and pass it to NewClientFromConfig via config_util. Some directly use NewTLSConfig:\\n- discovery/triton/triton.go (line 154): tls, err := config.NewTLSConfig(&conf.TLSConfig)\\n- discovery/openstack/openstack.go (line 197): tls, err := config.NewTLSConfig(&conf.TLSConfig)\\n- discovery/aws/ec2.go, discovery/consul/consul.go, discovery/http/http.go and others use HTTPClientConfig\\n\\n**5.
